    ENTRY["__main__"] --> PARSER["argparse parser (global)"]
    PARSER --> MAIN["main()"]
    MAIN --> FIND["find_modules(module_path)"]
    FIND --> WALK1["os.walk(module_path)"]
    WALK1 --> DECIDE1{"tf_files exist and\nlen(subdirs) > 1?"}
    DECIDE1 -->|yes| CMD1["os.system: cd current_path && terraform get -update=true && terraform fmt"]
    DECIDE1 -->|no| CONT1["continue walking"]
    MAIN -.-> CHECK["check_directory(directory_path) (defined but unused)"]
    CHECK --> WALK2["os.walk(directory_path)"]
    WALK2 --> DECIDE2{".terraform in root?"}
    DECIDE2 -->|yes| SKIP["skip"]
    DECIDE2 -->|no| TF_CHECK{"any .tf files in fnames?"}
    TF_CHECK -->|yes| CMD2["os.system: cd root && terraform get -update=true && terraform fmt"]
    TF_CHECK -->|no| SKIP

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant User
    participant Script
    participant ArgParser
    participant Main
    participant Finder
    participant OS
    participant Glob
    participant Shell
    User->>Script: run script with --path
    Script->>ArgParser: configure parser and parse args
    ArgParser-->>Script: args.path
    Script->>Main: call main(args)
    Main->>Finder: find_modules(path)
    Finder->>OS: os.walk(module_path)
    OS-->>Finder: current_path, subdirs, files
    Finder->>Glob: glob(current_path/*.tf)
    Glob-->>Finder: tf_files
    alt tf_files and len(subdirs) > 1
        Finder->>Shell: os.system -> cd current_path && terraform get -update=true && terraform fmt
    end
```

```mermaid
stateDiagram
    [*] --> Traversing
    Traversing --> CheckingRoot: os.walk root
    CheckingRoot --> Skipped: root contains .terraform
    CheckingRoot --> CheckTFFiles: root does not contain .terraform
    CheckTFFiles --> RunTerraform: .tf files present and subdirs > 1
    CheckTFFiles --> Traversing: no .tf files
    RunTerraform --> Traversing
    Traversing --> [*]
```
